# Yex Technical Document Section 0

## Overview of 11bcc1
This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 0.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 11bcc1_0

### API Reference: Method_1
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 1ms latency.

This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 726.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 236a81_726

### API Reference: Method_727
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 727ms latency.

This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 1568.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 9a79a2_1568

### API Reference: Method_1569
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 1569ms latency.

This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 1708.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 500721_1708

### API Reference: Method_1709
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 1709ms latency.

This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 1848.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 565d4d_1848

### API Reference: Method_1849
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 1849ms latency.
